### syncDevices()

```ts
function syncDevices<T, U>(params?: {
  type: T
}): (
  target: (...args: any[]) => Promise<U>,
  _context: ClassMethodDecoratorContext<
    unknown,
    (this: unknown, ...args: any) => any
  >,
```
